>python hanoi.py -h
usage: hanoi.py [-h] n

Solves Tower of Hanoi for n disks.

positional arguments:
  n           number of disks

optional arguments:
  -h, --help  show this help message and exit

>python hanoi.py a
usage: hanoi.py [-h] n
hanoi.py: error: argument n: invalid int value: 'a'

>python hanoi.py -1
error: n must be greater than 0

>python hanoi.py 0
error: n must be greater than 0

>python hanoi.py 20
error: n must be less than 16.

>python hanoi.py 5
Note: The maximum default recursion limit is 1000
